# Security Audit: Missing Authentication Middleware in HTTP Handlers

## Your Task

Find Go source files in the Loki and Mimir repositories that register HTTP handlers or routes without applying authentication middleware such as `middleware.AuthenticateUser`.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the security domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec` (grafana/grafana)
- `sg-evals/grafana-loki` (grafana/loki)
- `sg-evals/grafana-mimir` (grafana/mimir)

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

10-usertext-
Search the /workspace/grafana--26d36ec repository for Go files that register HTTP handlers or routes without authentication middleware.

Look for patterns like:
- .HandleFunc() or .Handle() calls
- .Post(), .Get(), .Put(), .Delete() calls
- router.Route() calls
- http.HandleFunc() calls

Also look for authentication middleware patterns like:
- middleware.AuthenticateUser
- middleware.Authentication
- middleware.Authenticate

Search for files that have handler registration but NOT authentication middleware applied.

Focus on:
1. Finding where handlers are registered
2. Checking if authentication middleware is applied to those routes
3. Identifying handlers that appear to be public/unauthenticated routes

Use grep patterns like:
- "HandleFunc\|Route\|Post\|Get\|Delete\|Put" to find handler registrations
- "AuthenticateUser\|middleware.Auth" to find auth middleware

Look in common API route files and handler registration locations. Start with searching for files containing handler registration patterns.

    19→	// Get adds a list of handlers to a given route with a GET HTTP verb
    20→	Get(string, ...web.Handler)
    21→

    23→	Post(string, ...web.Handler)
    24→

    26→	Delete(string, ...web.Handler)
    27→

    29→	Put(string, ...web.Handler)
    30→
    31→	// Patch adds a list of handlers to a given route with a PATCH HTTP verb
    32→	Patch(string, ...web.Handler)
    33→
    34→	// Any adds a list of handlers to a given route with any HTTP verb
    35→	Any(string, ...web.Handler)
    36→
    37→	// Group allows you to pass a function that can add multiple routes
    38→	// with a shared prefix route.
    39→	Group(string, func(RouteRegister), ...web.Handler)

    41→	// Insert adds more routes to an existing Group.
    42→	Insert(string, func(RouteRegister), ...web.Handler)
    43→
    44→	// Register iterates over all routes added to the RouteRegister

     9→
    10→func (hs *HTTPServer) databaseHealthy(ctx context.Context) bool {
    11→	const cacheKey = "db-healthy"
    12→
    13→	if cached, found := hs.CacheService.Get(cacheKey); found {
    14→		return cached.(bool)
    15→	}
    16→
    17→	err := hs.SQLStore.WithDbSession(ctx, func(session *db.Session) error {
    18→		_, err := session.Query("SELECT 1")
    19→		return err
    20→	})
    21→	healthy := err == nil
    22→
    23→	hs.CacheService.Set(cacheKey, healthy, time.Second*5)
    24→	return healthy
    25→}

    18→func (hs *HTTPServer) OAuthLogin(reqCtx *contextmodel.ReqContext) {
    19→	name := web.Params(reqCtx.Req)[":name"]
    20→
    21→	if errorParam := reqCtx.Query("error"); errorParam != "" {
    22→		errorDesc := reqCtx.Query("error_description")
    23→		hs.log.Error("failed to login ", "error", errorParam, "errorDesc", errorDesc)
    24→		hs.redirectWithError(reqCtx, errutil.Unauthorized("oauth.login", errutil.WithPublicMessage(hs.Cfg.OAuthLoginErrorMessage)).Errorf("Login provider denied login request"))
    25→		return
    26→	}
    27→
    28→	code := reqCtx.Query("code")
    29→	redirectTo := reqCtx.Query("redirectTo")
    30→
    31→	req := &authn.Request{HTTPRequest: reqCtx.Req}

## Summary

I've completed a comprehensive analysis of the Grafana repository at `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec` for HTTP handlers registered without proper authentication middleware. Here are my findings:

### Key Analysis Files:
1. **Main Routing**: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/api.go` (registerRoutes function)
2. **Route Registration Logic**: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/routing/route_register.go`
3. **Middleware Definitions**: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/middleware/auth.go`

### Handlers Found Without Authentication Middleware:

**Total Routes Without Explicit Auth Middleware: 23**

Most are intentionally public (by design):
- Login/Logout endpoints
- Signup/Password reset flows
- Public/snapshot viewing
- Avatar/Gravatar services
- Public plugin assets
- OAuth callbacks

### Critical Finding - Security Concerns:

Two routes that SHOULD have explicit authentication middleware but don't at the route registration level:

1. **Line 245 in api.go**: 
   ```go
   r.Post("/api/user/auth-tokens/rotate", routing.Wrap(hs.RotateUserAuthToken))
   ```
   - Handler file: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/user_token.go:110`
   - Missing: `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware
   - Issue: Relies on handler-level checks only

2. **Line 246 in api.go**:
   ```go
   r.Get("/user/auth-tokens/rotate", routing.Wrap(hs.RotateUserAuthTokenRedirect))
   ```
   - Handler file: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/user_token.go:78`
   - Missing: `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware
   - Issue: Relies on handler-level checks only

Both handlers do perform authentication checks internally (token validation, cookie checks), but they lack explicit middleware enforcement for defense-in-depth security practices used

## Summary

**Status**: I encountered a critical limitation in completing this task.

**Issue**: The Loki and Mimir repositories specified in the task are not available in the local workspace. The workspace only contains the Grafana repository (`/workspace/grafana--26d36ec`). While the task mentions these repositories are "accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools," those tools are not available in my current environment.

**What I found**:
- The Grafana repository contains extensive HTTP API handler registrations in `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/api.go`
- Grafana uses a middleware system with functions like `reqSignedIn`, `reqSignedInNoAnonymous`, and `authorize()` to protect routes
- One potential issue identified in Grafana (lines 245-246): Auth token rotation endpoints registered without explicit middleware, though the handlers implement authentication internally

**Limitation**: These findings are from **Grafana**, not Loki or Mimir as required by the task specification.

**To complete the audit**, the Loki and Mimir repositories would need to be:
1. Available in the workspace filesystem, OR
2. Accessible through functional Sourcegraph MCP tools

Handler returns 401 Unauthorized if token validation fails\n      - Handler expects valid session/token cookies\n    - **POTENTIAL SECURITY CONCERN**: Should have explicit `reqSignedIn` middleware\n    - Recommendation: Add `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware\n\n23. **Line 246**: `r.Get(\"/user/auth-tokens/rotate\", routing.Wrap(hs.RotateUserAuthTokenRedirect))`\n    - NO MIDDLEWARE DEFINED AT ROUTE LEVEL\n    - Handler: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/user_token.go:78`\n    - Issue: Route has NO authentication middleware registered\n    - Handler Analysis: The handler calls `hs.rotateToken(c)` which gets cookie value\n      - If no valid token in cookie, returns redirect to login\n      - Does perform token validation\n    - **POTENTIAL SECURITY CONCERN**: Should have explicit `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware\n    - Recommendation: Add `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware\n\n---\n\n## Authentication Middleware Patterns Found\n\n### Defined Middleware (in api.go):\n- `reqNoAuth := middleware.NoAuth()` (Line 63)\n- `reqSignedIn := middleware.ReqSignedIn` (Line 64)\n- `reqNotSignedIn := middleware.ReqNotSignedIn` (Line 65)\n- `reqSignedInNoAnonymous := middleware.ReqSignedInNoAnonymous` (Line 66)\n- `reqGrafanaAdmin := middleware.ReqGrafanaAdmin` (Line 67)\n- `reqOrgAdmin := middleware.ReqOrgAdmin` (Line 68)\n- `authorize := ac.Middleware(hs.AccessControl)` (Line 73)\n\n### Middleware Definitions (middleware/middleware.go, middleware/auth.go):\n- `ReqGrafanaAdmin` - Requires Grafana admin role\n- `ReqSignedIn` - Requires user to be signed in\n- `ReqSignedInNoAnonymous` - Requires signed in, no anonymous users\n- `ReqEditorRole` - Requires editor role or higher\n- `ReqOrgAdmin` - Requires org admin role\n- `NoAuth()` - Explicitly allows no authentication\n\n---\n\n## Summary Statistics\n\n- **Total Top-Level Routes Analyzed**: ~100+\n- **Routes with NO middleware**: 23\n- **Routes with Explicit Auth Middleware**: ~60+\n- **Routes in API Groups** (with group-level auth): ~300+\n\n---\n\n## Routes Requiring Attention\n\nOnly TWO routes appear to lack proper authentication middleware at the route level but handle authentication internally:\n\n1. `/api/user/auth-tokens/rotate` (POST) - Line 245\n2. `/user/auth-tokens/rotate` (GET) - Line 246\n\nBoth should have explicit `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware applied for defense-in-depth and to match the pattern used throughout the rest of the codebase.\n\n---\n\n## Recommendations\n\n1. **Add Explicit Middleware**: Routes 245 and 246 should include `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware\n2. **Defense in Depth**: Relying on handler-level checks alone is less secure than middleware enforcement\n3. **Consistency**: Most protected routes in Grafana explicitly specify their auth requirements at registration time\n4. **Code Review**: Any new routes should follow the established pattern of explicit middleware\n\nENDOFFILE\ncat /tmp/findings.md\n",

# Grafana HTTP Handler Authentication Analysis

## Repository: /workspace/grafana--26d36ec

### Summary
Analysis of Go files in the Grafana repository focusing on HTTP handler registration and authentication middleware patterns.

---

## Key Files Analyzed

### Main Routing File
- **File**: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/api.go`
- **Lines**: 1-597 (registerRoutes function)
- **Framework**: Custom routing system using `routing.RouteRegister` interface

### Supporting Files
- `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/routing/route_register.go` - Route registration logic
- `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/middleware/middleware.go` - Middleware definitions
- `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/middleware/auth.go` - Authentication middleware

---

## Findings: Handlers WITHOUT Explicit Authentication Middleware

### Category 1: Public/Unauthenticated Routes (By Design)

These routes are intentionally public and do NOT require authentication:

1. **Line 81**: `r.Get("/logout", hs.Logout)`
   - NO MIDDLEWARE - Public logout endpoint
   - Handler: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/login.go:309`
   - Status: Expected - user must be able to logout

2. **Line 85**: `r.Get("/login", hs.LoginView)`
   - NO MIDDLEWARE - Login page
   - Handler: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/login.go:112`
   - Status: Expected - users need to access login

3. **Line 86**: `r.Get("/invite/:code", hs.Index)`
   - NO MIDDLEWARE - Invitation endpoint
   - Status: Accepts code parameter for user invitations

4. **Line 95**: `r.Get("/.well-known/change-password", redirectToChangePassword)`
   - NO MIDDLEWARE - Standard .well-known endpoint
   - Status: Public standard path

### Category 5: Protected Routes - REQUIRES ATTENTION

22. **Line 245**: `r.Post("/api/user/auth-tokens/rotate", routing.Wrap(hs.RotateUserAuthToken))`
    - NO MIDDLEWARE DEFINED AT ROUTE LEVEL
    - Handler: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/user_token.go:110`
    - Issue: Route has NO authentication middleware registered
    - Handler Analysis: The handler DOES check authentication internally via `c.GetInternalID()` 
      - Handler returns 401 Unauthorized if token validation fails
      - Handler expects valid session/token cookies
    - **POTENTIAL SECURITY CONCERN**: Should have explicit `reqSignedIn` middleware
    - Recommendation: Add `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware

23. **Line 246**: `r.Get("/user/auth-tokens/rotate", routing.Wrap(hs.RotateUserAuthTokenRedirect))`
    - NO MIDDLEWARE DEFINED AT ROUTE LEVEL
    - Handler: `/workspace/grafana--26d36ec/pkg/api/user_token.go:78`
    - Issue: Route has NO authentication middleware registered
    - Handler Analysis: The handler calls `hs.rotateToken(c)` which gets cookie value
      - If no valid token in cookie, returns redirect to login
      - Does perform token validation
    - **POTENTIAL SECURITY CONCERN**: Should have explicit `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware
    - Recommendation: Add `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware

---

## Authentication Middleware Patterns Found

### Defined Middleware (in api.go):
- `reqNoAuth := middleware.NoAuth()` (Line 63)
- `reqSignedIn := middleware.ReqSignedIn` (Line 64)
- `reqNotSignedIn := middleware.ReqNotSignedIn` (Line 65)
- `reqSignedInNoAnonymous := middleware.ReqSignedInNoAnonymous` (Line 66)
- `reqGrafanaAdmin := middleware.ReqGrafanaAdmin` (Line 67)
- `reqOrgAdmin := middleware.ReqOrgAdmin` (Line 68)
- `authorize := ac.Middleware(hs.AccessControl)` (Line 73)

### Middleware Definitions (middleware/middleware.go, middleware/auth.go):
- `ReqGrafanaAdmin` - Requires Grafana admin role
- `ReqSignedIn` - Requires user to be signed in
- `ReqSignedInNoAnonymous` - Requires signed in, no anonymous users
- `ReqEditorRole` - Requires editor role or higher
- `ReqOrgAdmin` - Requires org admin role
- `NoAuth()` - Explicitly allows no authentication

---

## Summary Statistics

- **Total Top-Level Routes Analyzed**: ~100+
- **Routes with NO middleware**: 23
- **Routes with Explicit Auth Middleware**: ~60+
- **Routes in API Groups** (with group-level auth): ~300+

---

## Routes Requiring Attention

Only TWO routes appear to lack proper authentication middleware at the route level but handle authentication internally:

1. `/api/user/auth-tokens/rotate` (POST) - Line 245
2. `/user/auth-tokens/rotate` (GET) - Line 246

Both should have explicit `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware applied for defense-in-depth and to match the pattern used throughout the rest of the codebase.

---

## Recommendations

1. **Add Explicit Middleware**: Routes 245 and 246 should include `reqSignedInNoAnonymous` middleware
2. **Defense in Depth**: Relying on handler-level checks alone is less secure than middleware enforcement
3. **Consistency**: Most protected routes in Grafana explicitly specify their auth requirements at registration time
4. **Code Review**: Any new routes should follow the established pattern of explicit middleware
